< review>
I have over 20 various fruit trees on drip irrigation, planted within the last 2 1/2 months on my 3/4 acre Carlsbad property. ALL are thriving, with the exception of two Fuerte avocado trees I purchased from Oceanside Evergreen Nursery at the end of July 2013. Of the 7 avocados I have, these 2 avocado trees started wilting, and the leaves started turning brown almost immediately. The bark now has greyish streaks & all leaves limp & dark brown, but still on the tree. One tree is now officially on the brink of death & the other not far behind. My research points to "Verticillium wilt"

I have checked methodically to assure all trees had proper planting, mulch, and water according to the California Avocado Association. Again, ALL other fruit trees including 5 other avocado trees (bought at Maddock Nursery in Fallbrook) are doing Fantastic! A side note: I lived 3 years on rental property in Fallbrook CA, which had an acre of Avocado trees that I took care of.  NONE DIED or became sick!

I just got off the phone & was told by Evergreen Nursery, they DO NOT GUARANTEE ANY OF THEIR TREES OR PLANTS!!!! BEWARE!  Apparently, they are not only selling diseased Avocado trees, they DO NOT stand behind their product either! I can state THIS guarantee..... I will NOT be purchasing any more plants from them, & will be removing  these diseased trees immediately before they infect the rest of my new crop!

It would be better to pay a couple of dollars extra at a reputable plant nursery, that guarantees their plants & trees.</review>
